<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 7; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(7);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

<div style="padding-left: 10em; padding-bottom: 1em;" id="dvReportFilters"><script>
    function OnFilterNameChanged() {
        var filterName = $('#FilterName').data("kendoDropDownList").text();
        $('#ReportFilterName').val(filterName);

        FilterName_OnChange();
    }

    function SaveReportFilterClick(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var fn = $('#FilterName').data("kendoDropDownList").text();

        var kendoWindow = $("#popupWindowReportFilterSaveAs").kendoWindow({
            content: { url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/ReportFilterSaveAs?" + "filterName=" + fn + "&amp;saveAs=0"   },
            modal: true,
            Draggable: true,
            refresh: function (e) { e.sender.title('Filter Save'); e.sender.center(); }

        });

        kendoWindow.data("kendoWindow").center().open();
    }

    function ClearReportFilterClick(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $('#FilterName').data("kendoDropDownList").select(0);
        ClearFilter();
    }

    function splitButtonClick_ReportFilter(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        if (e.id == "btnDeleteFilter__ReportFilter") {

            var fn = $('#FilterName').data("kendoDropDownList").text();

            if (fn== '[Unnamed Settings]') {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Default filter cannot be deleted.", null);
                return;
            }
            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete current filter?", DeleteReportFilter);

        }
        else
        {
            var fn = $('#FilterName').data("kendoDropDownList").text();
            var kendoWindow = $("#popupWindowReportFilterSaveAs").kendoWindow({
                content: { url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/ReportFilterSaveAs?" + "filterName=" + fn + "&amp;saveAs=1" },
                modal: true,
                Draggable: true,
                refresh: function (e) { e.sender.title('Filter Save As'); e.sender.center(); }

            });
            kendoWindow.data("kendoWindow").center().open();
        }

    }

    function DeleteReportFilter() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var isFilterReport = false;

        var IsGridDisplaySetting = $("#IsGridDisplaySetting").val();

        if (IsGridDisplaySetting != null || IsGridDisplaySetting !== undefined || IsGridDisplaySetting == true) {
            isFilterReport = true;
        }

        var fn = $('#FilterName').data("kendoDropDownList").value();
        var data = { filterId: fn, IsReportFilter: isFilterReport };
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/DeleteNamedFilter",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {

                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    LoadReportFilters();
                    FilterName_OnChange();
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });

    };
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var saveInProgress = 0;
    function StarImageClick() {
        showSpinner();
        if (saveInProgress == 1) {
            return;
        }
        saveInProgress = 1;
        var isFavorite;
        var reportName = $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text();

        icon = $('#starImage');
        if (icon.hasClass("hollowStarImageClass")) {
            isFavorite = true;
        }
        else {
            isFavorite = false;
        }

        var data = { reportName: reportName, isFavorite: isFavorite };

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/FavoriteUnFavoriteReport",
            data: JSON.stringify(data),
            contentType: 'application/json',
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null) {
                    if (result.favoriteStatus) {
                        icon.addClass("starImageClass").removeClass("hollowStarImageClass");
                        icon.data("FINSUIAnchor").SetTooltipText('Remove favorite');
                    }
                    else {
                        icon.addClass("hollowStarImageClass").removeClass("starImageClass");
                        icon.data("FINSUIAnchor").SetTooltipText('Set as favorite');
                    }
                }
                saveInProgress = 0;
                stopSpinner();
                $('#starImage').bind('click', StarImageClick);
            }
        });
    }

    function ClearDBPreportParameterError() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
    }

    function GetReportNameModuleName(reportName) {
        if (reportName != "") {
            var arrParam = reportName.split('_');
            return arrParam[0];
        }
        return "";
    }

    function GetReportNameValue() {
        var ddlReportNameValue = $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").value();
        var arrParam = ddlReportNameValue.split('_');
        arrParam.splice(0, 1);
        return arrParam.join('_');
    }

    function ModuleName_OnChange() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var ddlReports = $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList");
        if ($("#ModuleName").val().length == 0) {
            ddlReports.dataSource.filter({});
        }
        else {
            ddlReports.dataSource.filter({
                field: "Module",
                operator: function (item, value) {
                    var arrParam = GetReportNameModuleName(item);
                    if (arrParam == value)
                        return true;
                    return false;
                },
                value: $("#ModuleName").val()
            });
        }
        ReportName_OnChange();
    }

    function ReportName_OnChange() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        $('*[id*=popUpAccountExpressionDialog_]').each(function () {
            var kendoWindow = $(this).data("kendoWindow");
            if (kendoWindow != null)
                kendoWindow.destroy();
        });
        $("#insertToDiv").empty();
        $('#dvReportParameters').html("&lt;div style='width: 60em; text-align: center'&gt;&lt;img src='/Content/Images/spinner.gif' alt='' /&gt;&lt;/div&gt;");

        var loadFilter = GetReportNameValue();
        var isLoadFilter = (loadFilter != '' || loadFilter != null) &amp;&amp; loadFilter.split('_') &amp;&amp; loadFilter.split('_').length == 1;
        LoadReportFilters("");

        var reportNameValue = GetReportNameValue();
        var reportNameText = $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text()

        var data = {
            modulaName: $("#ModuleName").val(),
            reportName: reportNameText,
            reportParameters: null,
            filterName: "",
            reportNameValue:reportNameValue,
            clear:false
        };

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/ReportParameters',
            cache: false,
            data: data,
            dataType: 'html',
            success: function (result) {
                $('#insertToDiv').empty();
                $('#dvReportParameters').html(result);

                var IsFavoriteReport = $("#IsFavoriteReport").val();

                if (IsFavoriteReport == "True") {
                    $("#starImage").addClass("starImageClass").removeClass("hollowStarImageClass");
                    $("#starImage").data("FINSUIAnchor").SetTooltipText('Remove favorite');
                }
                else {
                    $("#starImage").addClass("hollowStarImageClass").removeClass("starImageClass");
                    $('#starImage').data("FINSUIAnchor").SetTooltipText('Set as favorite');
                }

                if ('False' == 'False')
                    $("#starImage").show();

                var IsGridDisplaySetting = $("#IsGridDisplaySetting").val();

                if (IsGridDisplaySetting != null || IsGridDisplaySetting !== undefined || IsGridDisplaySetting == true)
                {
                    $('#FormDBReportParameters').find("#dvReportParameters").empty();
                    $('#insertToDiv').append(result);
                }

                $('#dvReportParameters').show();
                var IsGridDisplaySetting = $("#IsGridDisplaySetting").val();
                //This check is added for the Grid Display Settings
                if (IsGridDisplaySetting != null || IsGridDisplaySetting !== undefined || IsGridDisplaySetting == true) {
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        async: true,
                        url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/GetGridSettingDataViewInfo",
                        data: {
                            reportName: reportNameText,
                            reportNameValue: reportNameValue
                        },
                        success: function (result) {
                            CreateDataView(result)
                        },
                        error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                            console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        //TODO: this should not be hardcoded
        if ($("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "NPERS Wage and Contribution Report" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "NSSRS Staff Reports" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "Iowa Certified Annual Financial Report" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "KPERS Annual Report and Export" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "PSERS Reports" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "CDE December Staff Report" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "Colorado December Financial Report" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "NY ERS Retirement Report" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "TRS Retirement Report" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "STRS Contribution Worksheet F-496" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "PERS Contribution Worksheet" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "LA County STRS/PERS Report" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "EDD Quarterly Form DE9/DE9c XML Export" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "PIMS Staff Reports" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "STRS Contribution Worksheet F-496 (San Bernardino County)" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "STRS Contribution Worksheet F-496 (San Diego County)" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "Employer's Quarterly Wage and Contribution Report" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "PERA Contribution Report" ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "1099 Data Export"  ||
                $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "SSN Verification Report" ||
				$("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() == "VT WHT-436 Report"
                )
        {
            $('#btnReports__GRD').show();
            $('#btnReports__CPE').show();
            $('#btnReports__PDF').hide();
            $('#btnReports__XLS').hide();
            $('#btnReports__CSV').hide();
        }
        else
        {
            $('#btnReports__GRD').hide();
            $('#btnReports__CPE').hide();
            $('#btnReports__PDF').show();
            $('#btnReports__XLS').show();
            if (isLoadFilter)
                $('#btnReports__CSV').show();
            else
                $('#btnReports__CSV').hide();
        }
    }

    function FilterName_OnChange() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $('*[id*=popUpAccountExpressionDialog_]').each(function () {
            var kendoWindow = $(this).data("kendoWindow");
            if(kendoWindow!=null)
                kendoWindow.destroy();
        });
        var reportNameValue = GetReportNameValue();
        var IsGridDisplaySetting = $("#IsGridDisplaySetting").val();

        var data = {
            modulaName: $("#ModuleName").val(),
            reportName: $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text(),
            reportParameters: null,
            filterName: $('#ReportFilterName').val(),
            clear: false
        };

        if (IsGridDisplaySetting != null || IsGridDisplaySetting !== undefined || IsGridDisplaySetting == true) {
            data = {
                modulaName: $("#ModuleName").val(),
                reportName: $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text(),
                reportParameters: null,
                filterName: $('#ReportFilterName').val(),
                clear: false,
                reportNameValue: reportNameValue
            };

            $.ajax({
                url: '/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/ReportParameters',
                cache: false,
                data: data,
                dataType: 'html',
                success: function (result) {
                    $('#insertToDiv').empty();
                    $('#dvReportParameters').html(result);

                    $('#FormDBReportParameters').find("#dvReportParameters").empty();
                    $('#insertToDiv').append(result);
                }
            });
        }
        else {

            $.ajax({
                url: '/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/ReportParameters',
                cache: false,
                data: data,
                dataType: 'html',
                success: function (result) {
                    $('#dvReportParameters').html(result);
                    $('#dvReportParameters').show();
                }
            });
        }
    }

    function ClearFilter() {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var reportNameValue = GetReportNameValue();
        var IsGridDisplaySetting = $("#IsGridDisplaySetting").val();

        var data = {
            modulaName: $("#ModuleName").val(),
            reportName: $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text(),
            reportParameters: null,
            filterName: $('#ReportFilterName').val(),
            clear: true
        };

        if (IsGridDisplaySetting != null || IsGridDisplaySetting !== undefined || IsGridDisplaySetting == true) {
            data = {
                modulaName: $("#ModuleName").val(),
                reportName: $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text(),
                reportParameters: null,
                filterName: $('#ReportFilterName').val(),
                clear: true,
                reportNameValue: reportNameValue
            };

            $.ajax({
                url: '/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/ReportParameters',
                cache: false,
                data: data,
                dataType: 'html',
                success: function (result) {
                    $('#insertToDiv').empty();
                    $('#dvReportParameters').html(result);

                    var htmlContent = $('#dvReportParameters').html();
                    $('#FormDBReportParameters').find("#dvReportParameters").empty();
                    $('#insertToDiv').append(result);
                }
            });
        }
        else {

            $.ajax({
                url: '/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/ReportParameters',
                cache: false,
                data: data,
                dataType: 'html',
                success: function (result) {
                    $('#dvReportParameters').html(result);
                    $('#dvReportParameters').show();
                }
            });
        }
    }

    function LoadReportFilters(filterName) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var data = {
            reportName: $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text()
        };

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/ReportFilters',
            cache: false,
            data: data,
            dataType: 'html',
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvReportFilters').html(result);
                $('#dvReportFilters').show();
                if ( filterName != undefined &amp;&amp; filterName != '') {
                    var f = $('#FilterName').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    f.text(filterName);
                    f.search(filterName);
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function selectFilterName(filterName) {
        var f = $('#FilterName').data("kendoDropDownList");

        var reportNameValue = GetReportNameValue();
        var reportValue = reportNameValue.split("_");
        f.value(reportValue[0]);
        f.text(filterName);
    }

    function ReportParameter_OnChange(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $("#ParameterChangedSenderId").val(e.sender._optionID);
        ReportParameter_DoPostback();
    }

    function ReportParameter_DoPostback() {
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/ReportParameterChanged",
            data: FormDBReportParametersSerialize(),
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvReportParameters').html(result);
                $('#dvReportParameters').show();
            },
            error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
            }
        });
    }

    function RunReport_OnClick(e) {

        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ClearDBPreportParameterError();
        kendo.ui.progress($(".maindiv"), true);
        if (e == 'GRD') {
            var suppressSubTotals = $('#SuppressSubTotalsCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;
            var suppressGrouping = $('#SuppressGroupingCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;
            var fitToSinglePage = $('#FittoOnePageWideCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;
            var Showreportparametersonreport = $('#ShowreportparametersonreportCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;

            $('#SuppressSubTotals').val(suppressSubTotals);
            $('#SuppressGrouping').val(suppressGrouping);
            $('#FitToSinglePage').val(fitToSinglePage);
            $('#Showreportparametersonreport').val(Showreportparametersonreport);

            $("#ExportFormat").val(e);
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                async: true,
                url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/RunReport",
                data: FormDBReportParametersSerialize(),
                success: function (result) {
                    kendo.ui.progress($(".maindiv"), false);
                    if (result != "" &amp;&amp; result.Success === undefined || result.Success === null) {
                        $('#dvReportParameters').html(result);
                        $('#dvReportParameters').show();
                    }
                    else if (result != "" &amp;&amp; result.Success === true) {
                         if (result.AddToJobQueue) {
                             StartJobQueueNotifications();
                             ShowOkDialog("Job Queue", "Your process has been started and is now in the job queue. You will be notified when it is complete.", null);
                             setTimeout(function () {
                                 $("#btnReturntoReportScreen_ReportToGrid").click();
                             },
                                 2000);
                            return;
                        }
                        window.location.href = result.Url;
                    }
                    else if (result != "" &amp;&amp; result.ReportExists === true &amp;&amp; result.DataViewEditedResultId &amp;&amp; result.ReportId) {
                        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindow__ExportToGridWarning")
                         .SetContent({ type: "POST", url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/ShowExportToGridWarning?reportId=" + result.ReportId + "&amp;DataViewEditedResultId=" + result.DataViewEditedResultId })
                         .SetIsModal(true)
                         .SetTitle("Generated Data Exists")
                         .SetWidth(515)
                         .SetHeight('50%')
                        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
                    }
                },
                error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                    console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                    kendo.ui.progress($(".maindiv"), false);
                }
            });
        }
        else if (e == 'CPE') {
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                async: true,
                url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/GetGridReportUrl",
                data: { reportName: $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() },
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result != "" &amp;&amp; result.Success === true) {
                        window.location.href = result.Url;
                    }
                    else if (result != "" &amp;&amp; result.Success === false) {
                        kendo.ui.progress($(".maindiv"), false);
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Error, "error");
                    }
                },
                error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                    console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                    kendo.ui.progress($(".maindiv"), false);
                }
            });
        }
        else {
            //Add check here to check that the selected display setting
            //Then we will create instance of AptaDataView and call export method by setting cycle id
            var IsGridDisplaySetting = $("#IsGridDisplaySetting").val();
            //This check is added for the Grid Display Settings
            if (IsGridDisplaySetting != null || IsGridDisplaySetting !== undefined || IsGridDisplaySetting == true) {

                var dataview = GetDataView();
                if (dataview != null) {
                    var reportNameValue = GetReportNameValue();
                    $.ajax({
                        type: "POST",
                        async: true,
                        url: "/QAAutom/GridConfig/ApplyGirdFilterForReport",
                        data: {
                            gridName: dataview._dataViewName,
                            reportNameValue: reportNameValue,
                            filterName: ''
                        },
                        success: function (result) {
                            kendo.ui.progress($(".maindiv"), false);
                            dataview.SetNameGridSetting($("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text());
                            dataview.ExportToFile(e)
                        },
                        error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                            console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                            kendo.ui.progress($(".maindiv"), false);
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
            else {
                var suppressSubTotals = $('#SuppressSubTotalsCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;
                var suppressGrouping = $('#SuppressGroupingCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;
                var fitToSinglePage = $('#FittoOnePageWideCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;
                var Showreportparametersonreport = $('#ShowreportparametersonreportCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;

                $('#SuppressSubTotals').val(suppressSubTotals);
                $('#SuppressGrouping').val(suppressGrouping);
                $('#FitToSinglePage').val(fitToSinglePage);
                $('#Showreportparametersonreport').val(Showreportparametersonreport);

                $("#ExportFormat").val(e);
                $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    async: true,
                    url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/RunReport",
                    data: FormDBReportParametersSerialize(),
                    success: function (result) {
                        kendo.ui.progress($(".maindiv"), false);
                        if (result != "" &amp;&amp; result.indexOf("window.location.href") != 0) {
                            $('#dvReportParameters').html(result);
                            $('#dvReportParameters').show();
                        }
                    },
                    error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                        console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                        kendo.ui.progress($(".maindiv"), false);
                    }
                });
            }
        }
    }

    function CreateDataView(result) {
        var dataview = AptaFundDataView.DataViewManager.CreateDataView(result.DataViewId)
                     .SetBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action")
                     .SetDataViewParameters(result.optionalParameter == null ? null : result.optionalParameter);

        // divDataViewContainer is used as a placeholder for the DataView div.  It should contain 1 dynamically created element (and only 1 element).
        var newdiv = document.createElement("div");
        newdiv.id = "div" + result.DataViewId;
        $("#divDataViewContainer").empty();
        $("#divDataViewContainer").append(newdiv);
        $("#div" + result.DataViewId).data("AptaDataView", dataview);
    }

    function GetDataView() {
        if ($("#divDataViewContainer") &amp;&amp;
            $("#divDataViewContainer").children() &amp;&amp;
            $("#divDataViewContainer").children().first())
        {
            return $("#divDataViewContainer").children().first().data("AptaDataView");
        }
        return null;
    }

    function SaveReportFilter_OnClick(e) {
        var IsGridDisplaySetting = $("#IsGridDisplaySetting").val();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var filterName = $('#txtFilterName').val();

        if (IsGridDisplaySetting != null || IsGridDisplaySetting !== undefined || IsGridDisplaySetting == true) {

            var dataview = GetDataView();
            if (dataview != null) {
                var reportNameValue = GetReportNameValue();
                $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    async: true,
                    url: "/QAAutom/GridConfig/ApplyGirdFilterForReport",
                    data: {
                        gridName: dataview._dataViewName,
                        reportNameValue: reportNameValue,
                        filterName: filterName
                    },
                    success: function (result) {
                        $("#popupWindowReportFilterSaveAs").data("kendoWindow").destroy();
                        LoadReportFilters(filterName);
                        FilterName_OnChange();
                        ShowAjaxMessage('Record saved successfully.', "success");
                    },
                    error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                        console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                        kendo.ui.progress($(".maindiv"), false);
                    }
                });
            }
        }
        else {

            if (e == 1) {
                $.ajax({
                    cache: false,
                    url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/NamedFilterExists",
                    data: { filterName: filterName, reportName: $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() },
                    dataType: "json",
                    success: function (result) {
                        if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                            SaveNameFilter(filterName);
                        }
                        else {
                            ShowYesNoDialog('Override Report Filter', result.Message, function () { SaveNameFilter(filterName); });
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
            else {
                SaveNameFilter(filterName);
            }
        }
    }

    function SaveNameFilter(filterName) {
        var suppressSubTotals = $('#SuppressSubTotalsCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;
        var suppressGrouping = $('#SuppressGroupingCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;
        var fitToSinglePage = $('#FittoOnePageWideCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;
        var Showreportparametersonreport = $('#ShowreportparametersonreportCheckBox').prop('checked') ? true : false;

        $('#SuppressSubTotals').val(suppressSubTotals);
        $('#SuppressGrouping').val(suppressGrouping);
        $('#FitToSinglePage').val(fitToSinglePage);
        $('#Showreportparametersonreport').val(Showreportparametersonreport);

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/SaveNamedFilter",
            data: FormDBReportParametersSerialize(),
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != "" &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {
                    $("#popupWindowReportFilterSaveAs").data("kendoWindow").destroy();
                    LoadReportFilters(filterName);
                    FilterName_OnChange();
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                }
            },
            error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                $("#divDBReportsFilterSaveAsAjaxError").html(result.Message);
                $("#divDBReportsFilterSaveAsAjaxError").addClass("global_message error");
            }
        });
    }

    function RunCustomReportSample1Report_OnClick(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $("#ExportFormat").val(e);
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/RunCustomReportSample1Report",
            data: FormDBReportParametersSerialize(),
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != "" &amp;&amp; result.indexOf("window.location.href") != 0) {
                    $('#dvReportParameters').html(result);
                    $('#dvReportParameters').show();
                }
            },
            error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
            }
        });
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("#starImage").hide();
        if ($("#ModuleName").val() != "") {
            ModuleName_OnChange();
            if ($("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text() != "") {
                ReportName_OnChange();
                var delay = 2000;

                setTimeout(function () {
                    ReportName_OnChange();
                }, delay);
            }
        }
        if ($("#hdnReportName").val())
        {
            $("#ReportName").data("kendoDropDownList").text($("#hdnReportName").val());
            ReportName_OnChange();
        }

    });

    function FormDBReportParametersSerialize() {
        var data = $("#FormDBReportParameters").serializeArray();
        $("#FormDBReportParameters").find("[data-role='multiselect'][data-ismultiselectorder]").each(function () {
            var selected = $(this).data('kendoMultiSelect').value();
            var fromIndex = 0;
            for (i = 0; i &lt; data.length; i++) {
                if (data[i].name == this.name) {
                    data[i].value = selected[fromIndex];
                    fromIndex++;
                }
            }
        });

        return data;
    }

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/Reports/DBReports/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }
